County 2020 2021 2022

STARKE 40.6% 41.8% 40.1%

Statewide Rate 37.0% 36.0% 38.0%
Data Source: CDC Places. Statewide rates to compare against regional and county rates was sourced from BRFSS data. PR = parti ally 
rural. Rates are age -adjusted.Chronic Disease & Primary Care

increase in 2021 -2022.

low for Indiana.
